1)
God's Desire
Everyone, regardless of being male or female, has desires. We know that there is a wish. If we observe our human world, we see various types of people. Some want to become judges, some want to become entrepreneurs, and some want to become scientists; there are many different types of people.
God also has desires.
When we look at individuals, there are such desires, and when we look at nations, there are also such desires. There are countries that must prioritize political issues, and there are countries that emphasize economic, cultural, or religious fields. Each country is moving forward from various positions that prioritize different directions.
The same goes for the world. Nowadays, in the democratic world, there is a desire that "this should be the way," and in the communist world, there is also a desire that "this should be the way." We know that they are moving forward with such wishes. So, if God exists, what would God's desire be? God also has desires.
June 19, 1977, USA.
* The exact location could not be confirmed.
8   God's Desire
Then, how should the paths of individuals, nations, the world, and God be? We can discover this when we go out to the sea. No matter how vast the sea is, the water flows. The water flows according to the flowing currents. The whole moves according to that.
The air also flows. The air flows too. Today, it seems that New York in the USA will be hot without wind, but the heat and cold do not just center around the area of New York. It expands according to the overall density of the air.
When we look at human life, people living in the past lived in various ways, people living in the present live in various ways, and people who will live in the future will also live in various ways. Do you think so? In daily life, some people wish, "Ah, I hope today is lucky. I hope something good happens when I go out today." Isn't that right? From morning to lunch, through dinner, and all night long, everyone wishes for everything to be good. Also, when spring, summer, autumn, and winter come, they wish, "I hope all seasons will be unforgettable good seasons for me." Everyone wishes for that. Furthermore, in youth, adulthood, middle age, and old age, everyone has wishes like, "Ah! I hope it will be like this."
The universe operates based on principles.
When we look at it this way, the universe has fortune. There is a path. Does the universe move randomly, without any principles, without any order, or does it move according to order? What do you think? "It moves according to order." Is that really so? "Yes." Then, does the universe say, "I will go this way"? Does it say, "It goes that way because everything is predetermined"? What is it? "It goes because it is predetermined." Then, is the universe the center, or is some law and principle the center? "The principle is the center." That's how it is.
All beings have principles before they exist, and the results of those principles determine the continuation of existence. Have you all thought about this? When I was born, did I start breathing in or out? What was the beginning? "Breathing in." You think so, but how do you know? Do you know how you did it in the past? Did you know that you were breathing in like "hmm"? Did you know that? "No." Even if you say you breathed in, did you do it by pretending to do so, or did you do it naturally? "Automatically." Why does it happen automatically? Did you do it because you wanted to? "It just happened."
When you are born, do you close your eyes or open them? "I close them." (Laughter) Then, did I open my eyes when I wanted to, or did they open naturally? "They opened naturally." Did you receive education on how to breastfeed? "No." Then how did that happen? There is an invisible guiding principle, a guiding line. There is a principled path for all actions.
In this regard, we must understand that all actions do not occur by chance. Today, evolutionists say, "The universe has developed; it is a natural occurrence." But how does it occur naturally? How can it just happen as it is? Can it occur without a cause, motivation, process, or result? Motivation comes first, cause comes first, and then direction follows. Then, why does direction arise? Does existence itself consciously say, "I must go this way"? "No." Why do the eyes open? When the eyes open, do they look inside or outside? Why must they look that way? Where does that directionality come from? How does that happen? We can understand that existence exists to follow direction.
Therefore, from this perspective, the universe did not come into being without a cause. Although everything is said to be a natural occurrence, nature did not just emerge. There is a cause within nature. There is directionality within nature. Moreover, nature circulates and moves while pursuing results. It is either in circular motion or in tectonic motion. It must move with directionality. Do you think so?
Thus, it can be understood that it has developed into a completed object, gathered in complex directionality, and resulted in such outcomes. The universe is said to revolve because it is a matter of fortune, and history is said to develop and revolve as well. Spring, summer, autumn, and winter are all said to revolve. If we see it this way, why does every stage of evolution not revolve? Why must it only develop?
From this perspective, looking at the world of circulation, I think this is where the theory of reincarnation also arises. People return as animals, trees, or anything else; there is a relationship there. Electricity also circulates. Plus and minus circulate. It must revolve.
The universe is round because it engages in reciprocal actions.
An object that is solid and strong becomes strong when the process of cause and effect always circulates without difference. We can think of the notion that it becomes an object that lasts a long time. Therefore, we can conclude that humans must also comply with such a law of circulation. Since humans evolved from the earth and have gone through a process of evolution, it is not that they return to the earth; rather, the starting point of humans is not the earth.
Then, where did it all start? It started from an invisible personality, from a power that has an invisible concrete content. Do you see the principle? Principles are known through explanation; they are not visible. The principled things that can be explained without being visible have a higher dimensional subjectivity than the visible itself and possess internal power.
Therefore, humans were born from the invisible God and became visible beings, and then they all return to the spiritual existence that cannot be seen by human eyes. The cause and effect operate in opposite directions.
Everyone, why does this universe resemble a circle? That is the question. Why did it become circular? It cannot be otherwise. It must be that way. Why? Because the giving force and the receiving force are opposite; if they collide in a straight line, they will all disappear. Do you understand? "Yes." Therefore, in order not to conflict, the more complete it is, the more completely it gives, the more circular it becomes. If it wants to receive completely, it will also become round. This is the principle of the universe. The more complete it is, the rounder it becomes. However, when it becomes that way, it continues to be consumed and disappears. Therefore, it becomes smaller and smaller. (While writing on the board) Do you understand? The laws of motion are naturally that way.
The universe is round because it engages in reciprocal actions. That is why I like the Korean word "wonman" (圆满), which means completeness. There is a saying about a complete personality. Completeness means being fully rounded. Do you understand what I mean? "Yes." Do you want that? "Yes." Now, if there is a circle, would you like it to be a small circle or a big circle? "A big circle."
Why are men and women different? Why are they different? Men push like pistons. (Laughter) Women do the opposite action. They are static. When you go to a baseball field, what happens? I heard from someone who played baseball that when the pitcher throws the ball with all his might, the catcher receives it with a "swish!" When the ball hits the bat and stops, does it just stop or does it spin and stop? When throwing a ball, does it go far when thrown in a straight line or when thrown with a spin? (Demonstrating the throwing motion) "Throwing with a spin goes further." Bullets also fly while spinning.
So, the eyes are round, and everything is round. Is there any part of a person that does not resemble a circle? Have you looked for it? What is it? What is it? Have you looked for it? "No." How about teeth? (Laughter) They may seem sharp and pointed, but they are also round. Do you understand what I mean? "Yes."
The reason why the universe became round is… the sun and stars are all round. There is nothing that is not round. Surely, right? Moving objects have such a destiny.
How should our Unification Church develop? We must invest strength; we must sincerely give to receive in return; that is the principle. When you kick a ball, it runs away in proportion to the force you kick it with. (Laughter) Does the ball fall like this or like that? (Demonstrating the motion while speaking, laughter) It must draw a circle. Why? Because everything that acts has that destiny.
Everyone, when a car is running and goes around a curve, what must it do? It must go in the opposite direction, right? Is that right? At that time, it is dangerous. At that moment, it is closest to the ground. When we humans try to get closest to the ground, it is when we are going around a curve. Isn't that so? "Yes." Similarly, when God is going, when does God get closest to the earth? It is when going around a curve. We meet at the most dangerous places. It is the same principle. When it is uncertain whether it will fall or succeed, new cultures develop from there. It is the same principle.
When watching a movie, there are thrilling scenes that are enjoyable. Is that right? "Yes." Why is that? Why is it enjoyable? When children go to the zoo, they shake while riding on a horse that is standing still. (Imitating the shaking) Why do they do that? They do it because they think it is fun. They do it to enjoy. When they go to a dangerous place, they exhale deeply and say, "Oh!" When you go to a scary place, you exhale with a "huh!" This means you took a deep breath. Isn't that so? "Yes." Therefore, it means that the range of movement is large. Because the range is large, it becomes interesting. It means there is a lot of excitement. None of this is accidental. It all occurs based on the principles of the universe. Because humans are within such actions, human life must also draw a circle.
A person who can unite black and white people is yellow.
13
When we get old, do all Westerners have white hair? When we look at this, the changes in the hair of Eastern people cannot be matched by white people or anyone else. Look. As they age, their hair gradually turns gray, starting from a yellowish color. Isn't that so? "Yes." When children are born, they have yellow hair. Then it becomes black and then returns.
Look, that person was born with gray hair. (Laughter) Do you know the polar bear? Such people are surely descendants of those who were born in the iceberg, close to the Arctic. (Laughter) These people are surely from places like Norway or Scandinavia. Where is your hometown? "That way." Is that so? "Yes." Really? "Yes." Do you think so? (Laughter)
Geographically, southern people are black. Their hair is black, and everything is black. Nowadays, when we see black people, why are they good at running? Recently, black people have many world records in sports. When we look at white people, they have sturdy upper bodies. When they kick with their long legs, they cannot exert strength. And when we look at black people, their lower bodies are bigger than their upper bodies. So, they run well. However, when we look at Eastern people, their upper and lower bodies are the same. (Laughter) Is that true or not? Look. Therefore, the north and south must combine to become one. (Laughter)
When we think about it, I believe that only Eastern people can unite black and white people from a structural perspective. Recently, there was a black person who played basketball and was about my height. He was my height but could jump so well that he could put the basketball in from above. Westerners are tall but cannot move. What does that mean? It means the lower body is strong. (Laughter)
In jumping competitions, we lose to black people. Nowadays, if you look at jumpers in the USA, there are many black people, right? If we look at this, all the principles of the world are...
One side alone cannot achieve completeness or perfection. It is only through the extremes that one can say there is completeness or perfection. What is ideal harmony? It is not something that happens here. It is seen as ideal harmony when it comes together through a long distance, drawing a distant circle.

White people are paddlers from the Arctic. All white people are from the Arctic. They are products of the Arctic region. Right? And what about black people? They are products of the southern, tropical regions. Why does America have a problem specifically with black people and white people? White people say, "Blacks are not human." They do not treat them as people.

Look. White is a contrasting color. You need to understand that. White is a contrasting color. Therefore, wherever white people go, we can find a history of war connected to it. It means that they oppose everything. Do you understand? And black is a receptive color, a receptive nature. Do you understand? If you only receive, you will perish. If receiving is good, you will perish. Just accepting will lead to destruction.

Why did they paint this blackboard so dark? Why not white? Huh? If white people only liked white, then all schools would use white chalkboards. Black can reveal all colors; it is a good, fundamental color.

When the land is symbolized, is it closer to white light or black light? "It is closer to black light." Speaking of mountains, the high peaks are naturally white—because of the snow accumulation—while the valleys are naturally black. This is because decayed manure accumulates there.

Human warmth and deep emotions are more abundant in black people than in white people. White people are cold. That is the global consensus. Do you understand? Why is that? It is because they always have to resist the wind, which leads to that behavior. Therefore, they reject everything. As a result, white people are very assertive. This is how it is. Wherever they go, they explode. (Laughter) I am not saying this to criticize white people; I am speaking through natural laws. (Laughter)

The leaves in the valley need to be exposed more because they are covered and it is hot. They need to be revealed more. Therefore, in terms of emotional aspects, white people cannot compete.

From that perspective, should there not be harmony between black civilization and white civilization within the realm of white civilization to follow a satisfactory form? Since they cannot do that, Reverend Moon, being an Eastern person, comes to ask for cooperation. Just as ice needs a motive to freeze solidly, that is Reverend Moon's strategy. This is how I think. (Applause) Talking about this… Time has already passed an hour. (Laughter)

The universe must harmonize with its fate to exist eternally. This is how the universe operates. The universe is structured on the principle of circulation, and through the action of giving and receiving, the universe becomes round. A person with a culture that can give must be united with a culture that can receive; otherwise, both will perish and be destroyed. They cannot exist. I compared white people to the mountain peak, but white symbolizes purity, and purity symbolizes snow and height. Why is it high? Because God is so.

Then, is the mountain peak there because of the peak itself, or because of the valley? No matter how high the mountain is, all the stones that roll down will eventually go to the valley. Do you understand?

Where will the decline of Western civilization gather? It will gather in places like valleys, in Eastern civilization. Then, when will Eastern civilization be revealed? It will be revealed when it becomes one with Western civilization. It is the same. A valley does not unify only with itself; to unite with another valley, it must draw a circle. The mountain peak must serve to facilitate that back and forth.

Thus, when the world tries to unite, the conclusion is that white people must help Asia, the Middle East, and black people as the end approaches. If the eastern valley is Asia, then the western valley is Africa. America must do that. Today, why does America, representing all white nations, have to help Asia and Africa? Have you ever thought about that? Do you understand? "Yes."

If they can do that, white people will gain the privilege to stand in the place of God. Because they cannot do that, they have lost that privilege to Reverend Moon. (Applause) That is how the world will unite. That is the harmony of heaven and earth, the harmony of heaven and earth.

Therefore, the teacher intends to mix marriages among men and women of all races—white, black, and yellow. That is the extreme and the extreme. If that happens, when going to relatives or in-laws, if you take a Concorde, you can get there in just a few hours. You can go from one end of the earth to the other in no time. Now, taking a Concorde, it is too close within America.

What fun is it for a white person to nurse a white baby? But how stimulating it is for a white person to nurse a black baby. What do you think God would find more interesting? "A white person nursing a black baby..." (Laughter) God would surely think that way. What do you all think? "We think so."

You all like blue eyes, right? Western beauties are thought to have yellow hair, blue eyes, and white teeth. You like that, right? Think about the blue sea. When you go out into a sea like the Atlantic, everything is blue. If you stay there for a long time, eventually you might get tired of the blue color. That color can become too monotonous. If a small black boat is floating in such a blue sea, all attention focuses on that boat. Thoughts are entirely concentrated on that boat. "Ah, what is that?" It provokes stimulating thoughts.

If that black boat had a white mast, it would be even more attractive. It would be more stimulating. Then, if it also had colorful flags, it would be even more stimulating. You would forget all about the blue sea and become completely intoxicated by it. "Wow!" Do you understand? "Yes." That is wonderful. That is wonderful. (Laughter)

Reverend Moon came to white society, and many in the media are paying attention and making a fuss. Why? It is because I came from Asia. Because I am different from them, I automatically draw attention. This is natural law. It is natural law. (Laughter)

To Americans, it may look bad, but when God looks at it, it is like looking at a boat in the blue sea. As a yellow person, I appear like a boat among white people, like the blue sea, so when God sees it, He is bound to feel attracted to that boat. It is the same. So, not only should we raise a red flag, but we should signal with a red flag.

Everyone, think about it. Where do you think God is interested? Not in the blue sea. He is truly interested in what happens inside the black boat. You are on that boat. You are on that boat. (Applause) There, a white person comes out and does this, a yellow person comes out and does this, and a black person comes out and does this; in other words, people of all colors are coming out and doing this. Now, let’s think about this. What would be more impressive: a gathering of only white people shouting "Wow," or a gathering of people of all colors shouting "Wow"? "A gathering of people of all colors."

Look at me too. Why did I wear a red tie with a gray outfit? It is attractive. And what is this? What is this? (Pointing while explaining) Concentrate on all of this. Why did I put this on my chest? Because there is a heart… (Laughter) When women wear necklaces, they usually let them hang down, not stick them on. Right? "Look here." means "Look at my heart." "Look at my love." That is all it is.

Wouldn't it be nice if a woman's breast was attached here (to the arm)? Have you ever thought about that? God placed it on the chest because there is love in the heart. (Laughter) It is closest to the heart, to the mind. Therefore, it receives the love of the heart. Thinking this way, you cannot imagine how interesting the universe is. Have you never thought about such things? (Laughter)

Today's title is "God's Wish." I need to sell newspapers too. (Laughter) Everything that happens, no matter how much humans claim or make a fuss, will inevitably align with the rhythm that the universe's destiny desires. As long as there is no power to stop this, people will naturally comply, and those who follow the way of compliance will surely develop along with the pulse of the universe. They will exist eternally. No matter how much Westerners try to do as they please, it will not go as they wish. Do you understand? "Yes."

A wise person is one who wants to align with the laws of the universe.

Therefore, among Westerners, a wise person is one who wants to follow the laws of the universe and align with them. Those who seek to walk that principled path will remain extended into Asia and the cultural realm of the world. That is how the conclusion is drawn. Is there a nation or an individual that wants to perish? Is there such a nation? "No." Right? Then why do they perish? Why do they perish? Who causes them to perish? It is not me. It is the universe that does it. Do you understand? "Yes."

Humans in history can remain and develop by aligning with the laws of heavenly fortune. Who does not want to be a hero or a saint? There is not a single person like that. You all want it, right? "Yes." Do women want it too? "Yes." No matter how much they shout, "Yes!"… (Imitating. Laughter) Do they still want it? "Yes! (Loudly)" Only women can produce soprano sounds. No matter how loudly a man shouts, he cannot become a soprano. (Laughter)

Then why does everyone want to love God and pray together, yet some people perish while others develop? Why is that? It is because there is a difference in whether they align with the rhythm of the universe or not.

For example, there is a river, and you have to jump along it, but if you start jumping like this, you will fall in. Do you understand? "Yes." Therefore, people must have great thoughts. They must have great thoughts.

The time for jumping is short, but the time for preparation is long. That is why God is a great God; the time for preparation is incredibly long. They have not jumped yet. When the day comes to jump, they will jump high. Do you understand?

Do you know how much money and preparation it takes to make a satellite like Apollo 11? They have to create all the stars, saying, "This is the moon, this is the earth," and then call it space. They go from here to there. (Drawing on the board while speaking) They can go back and forth anytime. They have already gone back and forth. In terms of drawing, they have gone back and forth. (Laughter) Right? In terms of the Unification Church, it has become the kingdom of heaven on earth. In this drawing, we can say that the kingdom of heaven on earth has been established centered on the Unification Church. In your thoughts, the kingdom of heaven on earth has been established. However, putting it into practice is difficult. It is very difficult. Do you understand? "Yes."

Some people say, "The principles of the Unification Church are great, but oh, I dislike the actions of the Unification Church." Such people should die; they should die. Such people are doomed to perish. (Laughter) Therefore, we must take action and walk out like this. Shall we do that or not? "We will."

"Oh, last year there was a fuss about the Yankee Stadium event, and because of the Washington event, the teacher urged us to work hard, but now it’s all about selling newspapers?" they might say, but we do not know what will happen in the future. If we tell those who have not eaten, "Hey, eat," and they do not eat, they might get scolded, and even if they do not sleep, they might get scolded. Grow! Grow! (Laughter) If we do that, everyone will be happy. "Ah, that’s good." How long will that last? When the time comes, they will rather say, "I will sell newspapers. That is good." (Laughter) That is how it is. We must think that way. Only then will we advance.

The issue is to advance. If we can surely say that we will advance, then that is development. Then we will not perish. We must be able to see hope in that and be proud of it.

Yesterday, I went to Barrytown to catch fish, but I did not catch any and came back empty-handed. I was grateful for that. Why? Because I thought this way. They probably complained a lot to the teacher, saying, "Why didn’t you call us? Hurry up and call us," since they were all invited to the New York church but were not called. So they probably came back with a lot of greed, thinking, "If the New York church caught this much, we will catch even more." They probably thought, "We will catch more than New York church. We will be the best." (Laughter) If that had happened, God, in His love, made sure that they did not catch any fish yesterday. He wanted to teach them not to be arrogant again, even if they catch fish. If that had happened, they would not have been able to sympathize with the fish and would have tried to catch them all without that thought. (Laughter) If they think, "This is a good lesson," that would be truly wonderful. Therefore, not everything that is bad is just bad.

Tears may fall, but the heart is trying to rise. That is how it should be. If the heart falls like the tears, it leads to destruction. That would be the end. However, the more tears fall, the more the heart rises, and it leaps. Those who are oppressed should not let their hearts be oppressed just because they are being pressed. Even if the body is oppressed, the heart must rise. Then a revolution occurs, and a new culture is established. Do you understand? Therefore, even if our Unification Church faces opposition and the teacher and the Unification Church are struggling, if our hearts rise, we will establish a new culture that the world does not have. That is the principle.

A group that has entered a deep valley can climb to the mountain peak. Do you understand? "Yes." The peak is connected to the valley. There is no connection between peaks. The peaks are all connected to the valleys, so those who suffer are bound to succeed. That is the principle of the universe.

In modern times, the Unification Church is the first religious organization to be so deeply embedded in the world. The question is whether the Unification Church can climb up from here or not. Can we climb up? "Yes." How far? How far will we go? "To the end." It is not easy. Someone must go up and drive a steel pillar in, and then either build a bridge or create a cable car.
we have fallen into the valley, so we must rise from the valley. Is it easy or difficult to rise? "It is difficult." We have come down to the deepest valley of human history. The deepest valley... There has never been an ideology in human history as high as the thoughts we possess. Theism! There has never been an ideology that claims to monopolize all of God's love. This is the most difficult path in the world. We must understand that. Do you understand?

When a cable car is built here, how long do you think the line of people from around the world trying to go up will be? It will create the longest line in history. Therefore, the line of people wanting to see that will become the longest line in the world. Do you think so? "Yes." We are currently at such a construction site. Then what is Reverend Moon? He is the chief supervisor, the overall person in charge. (Laughter)

If you ask God, "God, have you worked hard too?" God would say, "Hey, you little rascal, no one has worked harder than I have." He would respond, "Because I am God, I am working tirelessly from the deepest valley of the world to the highest peak without taking a single day off." Up to the fifth ridge, many people can follow along. Up to about the fifth ridge, anyone can follow.

When women set out on the journey, they say, "Ah, what a beautiful place!" and dance to the rhythm, but as time goes by, they start to say, "Oh, oh!" That's how women are! God will talk about the memories. "No." And men, who boast that they will become heroes greater than Napoleon and that they will move the world, start off excitedly but from about the fifth ridge, they say, "Oh, if I keep sweating like this, I will die." They all fall off. "No." (Laughter) The lunch bundle that God is carrying, the food bundle is getting smaller and smaller. 

This is the wish of God. The water bundle is also getting smaller. It's a disaster. "If we keep going like this, we will all die." They think they have to live alone, regardless of God or anything else. "No." Therefore, at once, the men fall off. They sweat and get hot, and eventually, they take off all their clothes. They take off their clothes like this and... (Laughter) What kind are you? No matter how far you go, there is no limit. When you enter the mountain, you can only see the forest, not the peak. It's all forest, and the peak is not visible. This is a mess. It feels like you are going in circles, not knowing where to go. It would be nice if the peak were visible, but it is not. When you think about going up, it feels overwhelming, and when you look down, the way down is clear. (Laughter) Therefore, the foolish ones who think, "I don't know. It would be wise to go down," all perish. Are you not like that? "No."

You are different from your ancestors. "Today it will be hot again, but do we have to go? Let's take a break today." Isn't that right? "No." Then will you go? "Yes." Even if your legs hurt and you feel like you are going to collapse, will you still go? "Yes." Why is that "yes"?

As you get closer to your destination, you become breathless and feel like you are going to die. If God takes you, He will lead you on the most difficult path, a valley that neither Satan nor any wicked person can follow. This is certain. Therefore, those who are greedy to become heroes will all fall off. Those who are greedy will fall off. Do you understand?

Who will remain? Only those who are determined to say, "I will die to reach the top of this mountain," can reach that peak. Only those who say, "I will not retreat until death is before me," will advance. Even if they die, those who leave a will saying, "If I cannot go for these reasons, future generations should prepare to go," are not the ones who perish but are spiritually alive in their ascent toward the peak of the mountain. They are spiritually alive.

Even if they die, such people will try to guide the way, cooperating in any way possible. Then how many times must they be prepared to die? "As long as God does not die, I will keep dying and coming back to life, dying and coming back to life." This is how it should be. Do you understand? "Yes." Only such people have the possibility of ascending. Only those who have the heart to ascend have the possibility of ascending. 

Those who make a resolution to act and prepare everything with a determination greater than that of the dead or fallen can rise higher than them. 

What kind of person will ascend? Those who, even if they die, will leave something behind will ascend. You must understand this. You must leave something that can develop in the future. Do you understand what I mean? "Yes." Reverend Moon is also on that path of ascent. He is going today and tomorrow. Now we have ascended a lot. Now look. When we look down, the whole world is beneath our eyes. There is nothing to look up to. We look down. In that sense, we are in a higher position than anyone in the spirit world, and we have ascended to a higher position than anyone in this world. Let's rise until 1981. "Yes."

The Lord's Lamb Feast must be held in the most difficult place.

The Peak of Suffering 
No one likes difficult or painful things. There is no one who likes such things. A place accompanied by suffering is a place that abandons happiness, peace, and everything. When born as a human, everyone tries to move from the place of suffering to the place of happiness. That is the demand of our daily lives. 
If God is happy, all beings can escape from suffering. 
Suffering is not normal; it is abnormal. Suffering is not about rising; it is about retreating and going down. The time of suffering is the moment when the standard of existence is ignored and approaches the standard of destruction. Because of this position, no person or being desires it. 
Since we individuals are like this, if there is a master who created this universe, the master would be in the same position. If the central God of this universe is in suffering, everything belonging to Him must remain within the realm of suffering. 
Now, looking at our church, if the central teacher of our church is suffering, you too cannot escape from that realm of suffering. The teacher represents not only himself but the whole, so the whole stands in the same position as the teacher. This is the same for families, social organizations, or any sovereign nation in the world. 
Looking at the United States as a nation, even if the president does not suffer, we can see that some social organizations, families, or individuals within it are suffering. However, a president who does not suffer cannot escape the responsibility if his people or any organization is suffering. Therefore, when such painful things happen, the president must bear indirect responsibility and take actions to liberate the entire realm of suffering. 
In a family, there must be central parents and children, or in an organization, there must be a leader and members belonging to that organization. In the Unification Church, there must be a central figure and Unification Church members, and in a country, there must be a president and citizens. In the world, there must be a subject, and there must be people belonging to that subject. 
Now, in this light, which suffering should we prioritize? When considering the stages or differences of suffering, which is more important? In a family, even if a family member is in a position of suffering, if the central parent does not directly engage in that suffering and can oversee it and escape, a way to avoid that suffering can be sought. If we consider the Unification Church, even if you are in a position of suffering, if the teacher of the Unification Church is not in suffering, he can save you from all your suffering. 
Therefore, if the president of a country is not in a painful position while the citizens are suffering, there is a way to liberate them. Furthermore, if the central God of this universe is not in suffering, even if all the citizens under Him are suffering, there is a way to be liberated. 
However, if the central God of this universe is in suffering, what will happen? There will be no way to be saved. Who will save you? It is believed that without having something that knows God's situation better than anyone else, there is no way to escape the place of suffering. 
In this light, if the central God of this universe can rejoice and be happy, we can conclude that there is a way for all other suffering beings to be happy. Therefore, the problem lies in the fact that God must not be in a position of suffering. The conclusion is that we must not leave God in a position of suffering. 
God Carrying Out Restoration in the Peak of Suffering 
Now, from this perspective, what has placed God in the most painful position, the peak of suffering? It must be the fall of Adam and Eve. God is a Father, and we humans are His children, so the fact that these children fell directly connects to God. When Adam and Eve see themselves fallen, being cut off from God, ultimately from their parents, is physical pain, mental pain, and emotional pain. We can understand that these three pains are connected here. Therefore, when Adam and Eve fell and distanced themselves from God, we can think that they surely shed tears and struggled. 
From this perspective, we can present that the pain endured by our human ancestors due to their fall is the starting point of historical suffering. 
Now, what happened because of the fall of Adam and Eve? It means that God's sons and daughters disappeared. What happened next? It means that God's own body, the stage that should have been God's house, was severed. Then what? It means that God's love was violated. Therefore, the place of the fall is a place where God's sons are lost, where God's body is violated, and where God's love is violated. Ultimately, Adam and Eve were both God's sons and daughters and God's body, the practical stage of God's love. In other words, they were practical beings. 
For God, the fall is a place where He loses His children, then a place where He loses the position of a parent, and then a place where the position of a couple is shattered. 
However, Adam and Eve did not know any of this. They did not know well. They simply fell from the embrace of God, the embrace of their parents, and they may have felt physical pain, mental pain, and emotional pain, but they fell short of the overall pain of the situation. From this perspective, the emotional pain of God facing fallen humanity, the suffering that humans cannot experience and cannot reach, must be the highest peak of suffering. 
Because this was shattered, it must be restored. Therefore, you must now walk the path of restoration, and to do that, you must seek a position that can transcend the peak of God's suffering due to the fall. Before that, it is concluded that there is no way to resolve the source of God's pain. 
Now, how can you feel that? You may feel it conceptually when the teacher says this, but how do you personally experience it? For example, imagine a woman who has lost her children, her husband, and her parents. Then, let’s assume she has lost everything she had. What would that be like? What would the image of that woman be like? Even as a woman who is miserable, torn apart by her heart and wounded in every way, think about the pure position of God who has not felt such emotional pain. When such a blow reaches Him, how great would that pain be? How would it be? If someone has committed suicide today, would their pain be greater than that? 
In this light, if we can talk about suffering, then no one else can do so except God. From this perspective, we must understand that God is the one who carries out the work of salvation and restoration from the peak of suffering.

Dear guests, respected professors, graduating students, ladies and gentlemen! Today, July 1, 1977, is a historic day for the Unification Church. It is also a day that marks a significant milestone in God's work of restoration. Today, we are holding our first graduation ceremony at our Unification Theological Seminary. I would like to express my gratitude to all those who have come to this ceremony.

And to the graduates, I extend my warmest congratulations and thank you for achieving meaningful completion at this school. I wish for great joy to accompany you throughout your lives.

Today, you are bidding farewell to the professors and fellow students whom you love and respect, and you are leaving this beloved place of learning. I would like to take this opportunity to share a few words with you.

The world we live in today is a world of confusion and disorder. This is because people cannot determine what the true standard of life is, what the true center of the universe is, and what its essence is. This confusion exists in the lives of individuals, families, societies, nations, and even the entire world. We are living in a world where absolute standards and center points have yet to be discovered. In short, this world has not found its owner.

History progresses according to the law of cause and effect. The cause is always manifested in the result. If we sow seeds of evil, we will inevitably reap evil results. If we sow good seeds, good results will follow. The reason this world is in chaos and disorder is that it started off on the wrong foot. It began with mistakes. Because the master of evil sowed seeds at the beginning of history, we are now reaping the results of evil.

Religiously, this is referred to as the fall of humanity. What we call the fall signifies a departure from the original state. The result of the fall can be likened to a disease that has deviated from a healthy state. Due to the fall, the original standards that God had intended could not be realized, and this world has never recognized its true owner.

Since the fall is a departure from the original state, to return to that original state, we must turn in the opposite direction of the fall. For this, we need leaders and guides. As you know, to heal a disease, we need a doctor who can diagnose the cause of the illness and prescribe the appropriate medicine. Similarly, since our goal is to return to the state before the fall, we need leaders who can accurately identify the original cause of the fall, provide solutions for healing, and be able to save humanity.

Only God truly knows the cause and content of the fall. God desires for humanity to return to its original state. This hope of God must be fulfilled at all levels: individual, family, society, nation, and world. To accomplish this task, God must choose leaders. The restoration of humanity can be compared to the work of a doctor, so God must raise capable doctors and leaders.
You felt the need to establish a hospital that can train leaders. Throughout history, philosophy and religion have engaged in the work of training capable leaders and doctors for God. Through these leaders, God desires to guide different nations and cultures toward a unified direction for His ultimate goal. God is indeed leading humanity toward a singular foundational standard, a central point of unity, and an absolute, harmonious, and eternal subject. In the end, God wishes for humanity to be guided to the true owner.

To reveal His absoluteness, immutability, and eternal standard, God has sent the Messiah. He has sent the Messiah as a savior for humanity. The Messiah can be likened to the chief physician of a general hospital. He is the model for all saints and righteous people. He is the unique existence that cannot be replaced by anything. The Messiah is needed by individuals, families, societies, nations, and the world. The necessity of the Messiah is absolute. He is the absolute and certain guide who will lead humanity on the ultimate path of return.

The Unification Church and its ideology have established a global foundation for the work of the Messiah. Today, your goal should be to become true doctors and leaders who can represent the will of God and the Messiah. In reality, you must become the hands and feet of God and the Messiah. You have the privilege of being the first builders in establishing God's family, tribe, nation, and world, ultimately setting the original standard, revealing the central point, and becoming the subject of the universe.

Today, I earnestly ask you to inherit God's important tradition and to become true doctors and leaders who will live as God's representatives. Let us go forth into the world to save humanity and guide all people to enjoy complete restoration. Remember that you are called doctors and leaders of God. May God's great blessing be with you…. Thank you.

Good Day!
Good day! Just hearing the phrase "good day" seems to bring you joy. People always want to welcome a good day and leave behind a good life. This makes us feel that it is the wish of our lives. However, the problem is that no matter how good the day, the year, or the life may be, if I am not well, everything becomes futile. Therefore, the conclusion is that no matter how good the external world may be, it depends on me. Also, even if I am in a good position, I can only enjoy that goodness if the environment aligns with it; otherwise, no matter how good it is, it cannot last long.

The desire to leave behind a good life is our life's wish. When you wake up in the morning, you tend to judge all circumstances by what you see. If it is a good day at first glance, you will feel good. When you see nature, if the scenery is beautiful, you feel good. This is not just superficial. When nature is beautiful and the morning sunlight shines with it, the beauty of nature takes on a three-dimensional quality. When there are green fields and a river flowing endlessly, you feel something broad and hopeful.

Now, if such nature is left desolate, how dreary would that be? It may be good, but it cannot be enough on its own. We see that nature is good, the river is good, the sun is good, and the morning light is good…. However, just having eyes is not enough. Next, there is the sense of hearing; we have ears. If a symphony-like song comes to us, a beautiful song that can please the ears, it becomes delightful. Now, look here. If nature is beautiful and you are enchanted by it, and then you hear a natural music sound, a very beautiful music sound, will your ears go toward the sound of that music, or not? You will leave everything behind for it, right? Is that so? "Yes." Then what is better? Is it nature or music?

Why is the song good? Because it has the ability to resonate with all emotions of joy and sorrow, it can express everything in nature or give a feeling that flows deeply in the heart. Thus, we need natural songs. Isn't that right? That is indeed a pleasant thing. You too, right? After a week, when the weekend comes, you purposely drive two or three hours to a scenic place, turn on the radio, and have a great time. So, it is undeniable that songs are good. Isn't that so? That is indeed true.

Next, when nature is good and songs are good, if there is a fragrant smell, you will forget the sound of the song and nature, and just "hmm" while smelling. You desire that, right? Isn't that so? Then, are you satisfied with just having good eyes, good ears, and a good nose? Is that enough? Next, there is the enjoyment of conversation. If there is someone to talk to amusingly, you might say, "Oh! There is nature, but stop that! I am listening to the song, so stop that! I am smelling the fragrance, so stop that!" Is that how it goes? When there is an interesting person to talk to, your mouth becomes happy. Your mouth takes pride in it.

Think about it. Even if nature is truly breathtakingly beautiful, and the best music is playing, if you are sitting there intoxicated, if there are interesting words like poetry or lovely stories that evoke feelings deeper than experiencing nature, you cannot help but engage in those conversations. Isn't that so? When you speak, is it just your mouth that is speaking? It is not just your mouth. While speaking, your ears are happy, your eyes are happy, and then your cells are happy; you want to speak in a way that makes your whole body happy. Isn't that right? So, your attire moves, your body moves, your cells move, and all your senses move while you want to speak. No matter how you speak, if you do it quietly, it becomes boring. When you speak, there is a playful interaction, right? (Demonstrates action) (Laughter)

A good day is a day when all of human senses feel good. When we think about this, what motivates a person? The eyes are a motivation, the nose is a motivation, and the five senses are motivations. Therefore, we can understand that happiness and joy are related to the interests of the five senses.

The expressions we can show when we are happy can be seen through our eyes. It is revealed through the eyes. Reactions must be revealed that way. So, when the eyes are happy, the mouth is happy, the nose is happy, and the ears are happy too. Is that right? "Yes." Do your hands and feet just stay still? They also laugh and make a fuss. It is natural to play while laughing. Then, do you laugh alone? If you laugh alone, that is madness. (Laughter)

So, what kind of day is the day that the eyes like the most? That is the question. What kind of day is the day that the ears like the most? What kind of day is the day that the nose likes the most? What kind of day is the day that the mouth likes the most? What kind of day is the day that the hands and feet like, and the whole body likes? "Today!" Why today? Because you hear good words, it is a good day.

What is the purpose of women putting on makeup? Who studied that? When you look at makeup, where do they focus their skills? They focus their skills on the eyes. (Laughter) Why is that? Why is that? It is because the eyes are important. They are the windows through which everything can be harmonized. If the eyes are unattractive, it makes one feel very uncomfortable.

Next, who told them to put earrings on their ears? The ears need to be attractive. "Pay attention to your ears!" This is a warning. Sometimes there are nose rings…. (Laughter)

And when they put on makeup, you should know that the makeup of the nose is the most important for achieving beauty and symmetry. If you do makeup poorly, the nose can look flat. Try putting something white on it; how much taller does it look? That is why Western women never put white on the tip of their noses. They gradually make it whiter to make the nose appear lower and more beautiful. That is the way of makeup. Isn't that so? They fuss over the nose, fuss over the eyes, fuss over the ears, and then what? They fuss over the mouth, the lips. Women do this…. (Imitates. Laughter) That is for sure, right? That is for sure. I think that is a very elegant statement.

Then, where do they apply it? On the hands! Hands! Why do they do it on the hands? The hands have a sense of touch. The hands are important sensory organs. Therefore, they are included. Then, women wear clothes and also wear necklaces. I believe that Western women need necklaces. When I see Western women, I wonder why they walk around so exposed. Diverse Evangelism Methods 

And the people you currently have, the people you have evangelized, think of them as people who will leave quickly, so don’t wait until ten months; think of sending them all within three months. So secure all of this within three months. 

You should do something simple and special in your state. Carry a bell and walk around ringing it at midnight, or do something to wake people up. Blow a trumpet to wake them up, or knock on doors, or do something. When it becomes midnight, gather somewhere and do something to become famous. 

Then go to places with many people and give lectures. Joke around and socialize. Wrestle too. If you go to a park where there are many people, you can split into two teams and have a friendly fight. Create such an environment temporarily, and lead 100 or 200 people to exercise. It’s better to play like that than to sit still. Sometimes you can have such fun. You can do what you enjoy. Why can’t you? Why can’t you do it? Everyone can do it like that. 

Then think about how I can absorb the public. If possible, go to their homes. Get close and say, "Hey, I like you. You remind me of my uncle or my cousin, so I want to sleep over at your house." (Laughter) What do you think they will say? They’ll say yes since you’re getting close... If you say they remind you of your brother, would they say not to come? You can sleep over for one night, and in the morning, sweep the yard and do all the chores. Then they will invite you to sleep over again, and you can ask to come once a week. That’s the strategy. 

You can also evangelize while shopping. When you buy something, joke around. "Your face is really beautiful; you look like a handsome person. My younger sister looks like this." Say that. If you say they look like your younger sister or a relative, would they dislike it? You’re flattering them. Fishing Business Plan
If I buy you a boat, do you have the confidence to move it? Do you have the confidence to catch salmon in New Yorker? If I buy you a boat, will you push forward? Is there anyone who can do that? How about someone from Los Angeles, Dr. Dust? How much do you want to buy? Buy one. A boat, I mean. Buy a boat right away.

We need to lay the leading foundation to develop the fishing industry in America.
This year, we planned to make 50 boats no matter what… I guess we need to buy more. We will buy in Los Angeles, and then surely in San Francisco. Do you want that? And we will buy in Washington D.C. too. And we need to buy in Philadelphia as well.

We need to have all the boats. Why? Because it’s necessary. It’s absolutely necessary for the teacher’s strategy in the future. So when we call everyone to catch tuna during the vacation, we will have to bring them in somehow, whether by loading or carrying. Then, two or three members from each state will come and compete. So we will buy in Washington, buy in San Francisco, buy in Seattle, and then on July 29, 1977 (Friday), in Los Angeles, and then buy in Philadelphia, and where else is there a sea? New Orleans, Louisiana, and Miami… “It’s Tampa.” Why did you move to Tampa? Isn’t there a sea in Tampa? Is it close to the sea there? “Yes.” So when buying the boats this time, don’t buy them separately; if the teacher says ten boats, buy all ten from one company and distribute them. That way, we can buy them cheaply. Do you understand what I mean? We can buy them cheaply.

Now that we’ve talked about it, let’s decide this. How many feet will you buy? “72 feet…” Not that kind of boat. We are currently anticipating a small boat.

The boat I have now is 48 feet, but that’s too big. It can go far, but… We don’t need to go far. A 34-foot or 38-foot boat is the most suitable.

The boat we bought before, ‘Sea Hope,’ was $54,000, and that’s enough. Even for tuna fishing, we can just tow it without turning on the engine. A boat with an engine is likely to have a big accident. **The Core of Unification**  
Now we know that everyone is living in two worlds. The good side and the evil side, the direction pursuing the good world and the direction pursuing the evil world, we experience these two directions in our daily lives. All the senses we feel through our five senses, of course, and even in our conscience, we feel such actions.  
If there is no God, the realization of the ideal world is impossible.  
Humans listen to good things, see good things, speak good things, and act well as a standard of cultural refinement in daily life. The external world appearing as two worlds is a problem, but when we focus on the individual, we experience the conflict between the heart's person and the body's person in daily life. Now! When we think about this, if we say that humans were originally like this, it is a contradiction. If God exists and created such people, then ultimately, that God is concluded to be an imperfect God, and it leads to the conclusion of a God with two directions. When we look at such humans, and from the perspective of discovering our contradictory selves, the basis for saying "there is no God" becomes clear.  
In this view, if we say there is no God, then everything we desire, such as goodness or ideals, becomes unnecessary for us. Ultimately, it is impossible for our contradictory selves to overcome contradictions and realize a world of goodness and ideals. Since we are such resultant beings, it is theoretically impossible for that resultant being to reach an ideal state that transcends itself.  
From this perspective, if we say there is no God, then everything like an ideal world, a unified world, or absolute love becomes impossible, no matter how much we talk about it.  
When we see this… If you examine what you pursue in your heart's world in your daily life, the heart seeks higher things. Furthermore, it seeks an eternal value world, not just a momentary one. This is an undeniable fact. From this perspective, what do philosophy and religion pursue? It is merely a means to introduce methods that can realize human ideals in the world of the heart and body.  
From this perspective, if we think that everything starts with us humans, there is a possibility that a logic like Hegel's dialectic can be established in which development occurs in a contradictory environment. Now, can contradictions struggle with each other and lead to development? Logically, that is a contradiction. Pursuing the realization of ideals through such a process is logically impossible.  
From this perspective, we might also consider a means to discover a hypothetical God and seek a solution. Then, will it be possible to realize ideals through that hypothetical God? It may seem possible in some processual phenomena, but ultimately, it leads to the conclusion that this is impossible. In this view, God must exist absolutely. Without God, this cannot happen, but how do we discover God? If God exists, that God becomes the foundation that can solve everything.  
**We can know God's existence by seeing that humans have fallen into contradictions.**  
So philosophy has come to a state of giving up while pursuing theories to discover God. Religion has tried sacrificing everything to discover God, but it is still stuck without a clear discovery. Then, does only humanity need God, or does God also need humanity? Humans need God, and at the same time, God cannot meet humanity without needing them. The ideals of God and humanity cannot be unified. The love of God and the love of humanity cannot be unified. This leads to the conclusion.  
If God exists, what will He demand from us humans? That is the question. If God exists, what do we humans need from God? It must not be something common. Therefore, while we need concepts of God, recognition of God, and discovery of God, we must also recognize that something more is needed to establish a relationship between God and humanity.  
Now, in this view, what would that be? It is the knowledge that humans need from God, the money, and the power. What humans need is not needed by God. Here, the problem arises that we must discover the common points between God and humanity. If God exists, what are the common points that can connect us? What is the cause of this disconnection? This becomes a problem. Therefore, what is the issue here? We cannot deny that we humans are contradictory beings. This is absolute. This is truth and fact.  
Now, where should the common points of God and humanity connect? If this exists, where can it be connected from? What is the standard by which this can be connected? In this view, even if we humans had some common points, we became contradictory beings that could not reach that common point because we failed to fulfill the standard that could unite us with God.  
From this perspective, when we see that humanity itself is a contradictory being, if we introduce the idea that it has fallen short of some standard or has broken down, we can discover a theory that says God exists.  
That is why the word "fall" is such a precious word. Because we have fallen, we find ourselves in this contradictory position, and when we consider the very fact of falling, it makes it possible to say that God exists, and it allows us to acknowledge that we ourselves have fallen and broken down. (Writing on the board) Because we have fallen, we cannot help but be contradictory, and because we are contradictory, a perfect God cannot be in common ground with us. Therefore, the theory is correct. From this logical pursuit, we can affirm the existence of God.  
God exists!  
That is why we know that there are two worlds from here. Do you understand? "Yes." So the concepts of the good world and the evil world have emerged. That theory is correct. In this way, today’s materialists and communists can break down the barrier of "there is no God."  
**Religion is the path to find the ideal union point between God and humanity.**  
If God exists, He cannot leave incomplete humans as they are, so there must be traces of a path in the historical process that can lead them to completion. What is that? That is religion. That is why religion emerges. So what is the purpose of religion? It is to introduce the path to reach God's world. If we analyze religion, what is the essence of religion? What is it? It is to become good people. To become good people and to create a good world.  
So what is goodness? What is goodness? If goodness exists… As mentioned earlier, when we can approach a standard that can establish common ground between God and humanity, that can be called goodness. We can only deduce it that way. So what is the content of goodness? What is the content of goodness? That becomes the issue. What is the content of goodness? Is it working hard, or is it speaking well, or helping others? Is my sacrifice what achieves goodness? Religion calls for sacrifice… What is the content? What do you think that content is? That is the problem. What do you think it could be? It must be understood that it is based on love. When we analyze the essence of religion, it is all about goodness, but what is the core? It is that it is based on love. Then why must love be the standard?  
Because both the contradictory human and the perfect God demand that point of commonality, and since love is the only thing that can hold such content, we cannot help but assert love. This is the conclusion. Do you understand what I mean? "Yes."  
What is religion? It is the path to find the ideal union point with God, and since the common content is love, the conclusion is that only love can create a complete unity.  
**The purpose of religion emphasizing sacrifice.**

Why, why must sacrifice be emphasized? There are various reasons. When we consider the question of why, within our contradictory bodies… both are contradictory. When we consider the heart and body, which is more contradictory?  
You must understand that there is a difference here. This "body" does not like absolute sacrifice and absolutely dislikes meekness and humility. It absolutely dislikes yielding. Is that so? "Yes."  
That is why one of these must be subdued. It must be rendered powerless. So what happens if you weaken this? The foundation for the heart and body to become one grows. Do you understand? "Yes." This theoretical basis can be found.

Let’s return with tears 
This morning, I will speak under the title "Let’s Return with Tears." Young people in America may not know what tears are. Have you ever been hungry, or cold, or homeless? You might think you are far removed from such circumstances because everything is provided for you. Let’s see a show of hands from those who have never cried. You have cried, right? (Laughter) 
Human tears and God's tears 
The tears you have shed were shed for whom? They were all shed for yourself; you must have shed tears centered on yourself. Have you ever shed tears for others? You probably did that after entering the Unification Church. Did you ever do that before joining the Unification Church? (Laughter) In this regard, we can understand that there are two types of tears: tears shed for oneself and tears shed for others. 
When we think about the origin of the history of tears, where did it begin? When the fall occurred, Adam and Eve must have shed tears first. Then, who shed tears next? God must have shed tears. In this context, Adam and Eve shed tears not for God or for others but centered on their own sad circumstances. However, the tears God shed were certainly for Adam and Eve, who were destined to be expelled due to their transgressions. Therefore, God's tears were not for Himself but for others, for His children. 
Thus, we can conclude that one type of tear is associated with the sin of sorrow, while the other is a tear aimed at goodness. In this light, the act of shedding tears itself is miserable. 
The history of humanity began with tears 
In the human world, the history of tears began first, not the history of joy or happiness. God also saw the beginning of tears first. When viewed this way, both humanity and God are miserable. However, the tears shed by humans are perhaps tears that must be shed due to their own faults, but God should not shed tears. 
Thus, the history of tears has begun from the ancestors of humanity, and we must recognize that the platform of tears has expanded globally. This is an undeniable fact. In that miserable position, the history of war and suffering repeats, and history develops. At times, individuals suffer and shed tears, and families, nations, and the world also suffer and shed tears in a repeating history. 
Therefore, we cannot discard the history of tears. Thus, after grieving for oneself, for one’s family, for one’s nation, and for one’s world, there may be a path to return to a new world of goodness, but there is no way to return to the world of goodness without grieving for these. 
To walk the true path, one must overcome the peaks of tears of God and humanity 
Humans fell due to sin, and while they fell from a personal standpoint, ultimately they fell to the very bottom of the world. Now, how can a person who has fallen to the bottom of the world overcome this? To do so, people in this world must center on themselves, their own issues, their families, their nations, or their own claims, and they must overcome this world while grieving. The conclusion is that they must go in the opposite direction. 
In this light, it is certain that God, who looks at the peak of humanity as it is, will grieve from an opposing position. We must understand that God is always drenched in tears. We must recognize that God has grieved from an opposing position. 
So, where is the place where humans are happy? It can only be found in the path of overcoming tears. What must follow? There is certainly happiness in the place where one has overcome the difficult environment that made God shed tears. Why? Because the history of tears began between God and humanity due to the fall of the ancestors of humanity. That place is where tears did not begin, so we must overcome all the worlds of tears. It is a natural conclusion that there can be no origin of happiness without transcending that. 
This is the position in which humans stand. Therefore, we must advance by overcoming that position, and it is the destiny of humanity today to cross not only the peak of human tears but also the peak of tears shed by heaven. Thus, those who wish to walk the true path must overcome both types of tears.
