Now, you understand. A true member of the Unification Church is someone who sheds tears, and a true leader is someone who sheds tears. That is why, having fallen through tears, we must shed tears for restoration, not centered on ourselves, but centered on God and shedding many public tears for humanity. The more tears you shed, the closer you are to the heart of heaven, and that is a law of cause and effect.

So, where did the tears begin? If they began with the individual, then shed personal tears, and through the victory of those tears, they must develop into familial tears, and based on familial victories, they must progress to tribal, national, and world tears. Do you understand what I mean? "Yes." Until now, you have not thought about this. But now, after hearing the words, since that is the truth, from now on, those who will follow the heart of heaven with tears and shed tears for humanity, raise your hands. Put them down.

You must know how to shed tears for the figures of the restoration providence. 

So, what is the quick path? If you are Adam, then be able to shed tears in place of Adam; if you are Noah, then shed tears in place of Noah! That is the quick path. Replace the positions of Abraham and Moses. Then, shed tears in place of Jesus. Do you understand what I mean? "Yes." Through that, a bridge will be built. Starting from the individual...

God made Noah prepare for 120 years, placing the entire mission of judgment on him. The circumstances of Noah, who bore such a responsibility, and the circumstances of Abraham, who lived like a gypsy to lay the foundation for a new nation in accordance with God's will, and the circumstances of Moses, who was in the palace, liberating the Israelite nation suffering, and working for that nation within God's will, are not someone else's circumstances; they are my circumstances. At that time, did God not shed tears? Therefore, everything in the historical age was done for me, for me, for me alone.

For Jesus... who was Jesus for 33 years? He was for me, to teach me my path. How pitiful was Noah? You must be the ones who can shed tears for Noah. God did that. That is how God becomes a friend. When Abraham made a mistake in offering sacrifices, God was saddened. You must be the ones who can shed tears for him. Because God did that, God becomes a companion. When Moses failed, God shed tears, so you must be the ones who can shed tears in that scene. When Jesus was crucified, God shed tears, so you must be the ones who can shed tears for Jesus. Is that far from thought?

That is why today, in order to save such people, what has Reverend Moon of the Unification Church done? He has done such work. It starts from the individual. Here, I must tie together the emotional entanglements from the time of Noah to the time of Abraham, from the time of Moses to the time of Jesus.

Now, when you think of Noah's family, you must know that the teacher shed tears for Noah's family. If it is Adam's family, you must know what the content of Adam's family is and you must enter into the position of Adam. You must know the traces of the tears shed there. If it is Abraham, then Abraham; if it is Moses, then Moses; if it is John the Baptist, then John the Baptist; if it is Jesus, then Jesus. You must know the fact that there were tears that could not be spoken until you know everything.

Look. At the same time that there were tears to connect such historical standards, there were also tears to practice this. You must understand that tears have been shed through the individual era, the familial era, the tribal era, the national era, and the global era. You must tie this together and connect it. (While writing on the board) That is how it becomes a circle. 

And this is the spirit world, and this is the physical world. From here, it goes from Adam to Noah, to Abraham, and finally to Jesus. Here, it becomes Jesus. From here, it goes through the individual, family, tribe, nation, and state eras to the time of the Second Coming. It is the same. (While writing on the board)

Is that easy? Is that easy? Yes, it is great that we have discovered all historical failures theoretically in the Unification Church era, but how great would it be if we had woven this together emotionally?

When a spiritual person prayed about Reverend Moon, asking, "What kind of person is Reverend Moon?" heaven understood and caused him to open his mouth and weep. You must understand that. In this age, since you cannot go like this, you must shed tears for the teacher, using the teacher as a bridge. You must shed tears for God and the teacher.

The scariest thing is when God's love departs. 

Among those who have been in the Unification Church for a long time, many use the teacher, but there is no one who sheds tears for the teacher. That will all flow away and pass. I know many of such people among those blessed families in Korea. In order to save such people, I think that as the will is fulfilled more and more, they must be placed in the most difficult process once. They will repent of their mistakes only after entering the Unification Church and realize that they could not shed tears for the teacher, and then they will be restored.
318   Let's Return with Tears
When the old leaders appear before the teacher dressed in fine clothes, I keep an eye on them. When they show up in nice cars, I watch them closely. Do they qualify to drive that car? If they live in a good house, I observe them. Do you understand what I mean? "Yes." Now you understand. That’s why, for all of this, shedding tears and how much you have cried for God, the current Unification Church, and the teacher is the secret to reaching the heart of heaven.

If you love God and humanity as much as the teacher loves them, you will surely become the embodiment of love. Recognize the teacher's words as a historical declaration, and even if no one else keeps them, you must say, "I will keep them with tears, even until the next command comes." 

As the times progress, new commands keep emerging. New commands keep coming forth and rising. Some people think that just being here is enough, but that is not the case. You must struggle and put in effort here; if you can't do it, then give it your all, and that is how you will rise. You are meant to rise in that way. You have not acted on any of the many commands the teacher has given until now.

As a result, when new commands are given, everything just goes around in circles. That cannot happen. If you are trying to follow that path with all your strength and tears but fail to achieve it, that is what connects you.

Look. You are now here, in this time of progress, in this Belvedere, and you can see the teacher at any time, but internally, there is such a difference. (He writes on the board) Why is that? God and the teacher are anxiously working on this matter, while you are at ease. Last year is gone, and this year is the same. You have discovered it, but you have not become the owner.

In that case, the next people coming in will inherit this. Do you understand what I mean? "Yes." Why? Because the newcomers will work hard. But those who came first are blocking the path of those who came later with their signs.

If not, at least shed some tears. If you are ashamed to face the newcomers, then be humble. You need to recognize that there is such a tendency. This must be resolved. You should know well what kind of person you are. Do not cover that up; be honest in front of your family. If you cannot do that, even if you have been here longer, do not step forward. Even if you have become a leader, stand back.

The teacher knows that. I may not speak of it or handle it, but I know how to see, and I know exactly what the current situation is. Therefore, today, those who have been here a long time must repent. You must shed tears, tears. Do you understand what I mean? "Yes." Why are we doing this? Why must we do this? If we do not, God's love will depart from us. What is the most frightening thing? It is not the lack of money, nor is it the persecution and misery; the most frightening thing is that God's love departs. The departure of God's love is the most frightening thing. Do you understand what I mean? "Yes." The same goes for the teacher. The teacher is not afraid of money. I am not afraid of anyone or anything. The departure of God's love... We must hold onto that love until we die and live in this world. You must understand that no one can bind it or separate it.

Our Important Task
Now, knowing this, from this morning, you must think back on the past with that determination and reflect on when you shed tears for the heavenly will. If that is absent, you must repent immediately and struggle to follow that path. 

Who is the owner? The person who has shed many tears for New York, or for the worldwide Unification Church, or for all of humanity can be seen as the owner. It may seem miserable now and like nothing, but it will flow as living water for ten years, a hundred years, and even for thousands of generations. Through such descendants, the world will be restored. They will become the owners of the world.

This is like a large low-pressure system; a high-pressure system will naturally come to this place. So, when you go out into such a position, tears will flow. You will shed tears. Just like when a high-pressure system moves and a storm blows, bringing rain, it is exactly the same.

Therefore, you must feel, "Ah, I am the only one left. I am the only one remaining!" When you are in such a position and entrust yourself, your family, your nation, and your world to heaven, heaven will take charge. Just as I am lonely, God is lonely... "Above, God is alone, and on earth, I am alone, so I will endlessly work to restore the individual, endlessly work to restore the family, and as long as you do not disappear, I will not disappear, nor will I yield!" You must make such a declaration. You must make such a resolution with tears. Have you ever had such a time?

It is not about crying for yourself; it is about crying for humanity and God. If you make such a resolution in such a position and go through such a process until you die, you will undoubtedly become a beloved son or daughter of God, without a doubt. The conclusion is that God seeks His sons and daughters amidst such global tears. You must understand that outside of that position, God's true sons and daughters cannot be found in the heavenly kingdom.

That is why what I desire before heaven is this: "Heaven! Send me to the valley of tears!" That is my wish. "Send me to the valley of tears!" Do you understand what I mean? "Yes." You must become such individuals and resolve to walk this path anew from today. You all raised your hands and made a promise, right? You should know well what position you are in. There is no need for explanation. You all know, right? Do you not know? "We know." Therefore, the self that knows cannot perish. Since you know, you cannot perish. My body, I, as a person, am a common possession of the world, a shared item. You must understand that. You have the responsibility to wrap this up beautifully and with care.

If you walk such a path, many will come forth to shed tears for you. You must know that many such people will emerge. Not only people, but even God will shed tears. How much have you made God cry on earth? How much have you moved God to tears on earth? You must understand that this is our important task.

God has also been doing hard work until now. Therefore, there is no other way to take responsibility for the hard work God is doing and to walk the path while risking death.

When we look at it this way, who will be the owner of the world, the owner of the heavenly kingdom? Without a doubt, it can only be someone who has shed tears like this. If someone else becomes the owner, then everything I have said today is a lie. Do you think that is correct? Do you think it is true or not true? "It seems true." It is undoubtedly true. It is undoubtedly true.

True Friends and True Family
A true friend is someone who sheds tears for me. A true family member is someone who takes responsibility for their family and sheds tears for those who are in difficulty. Is that not so? You must become someone who can shed tears for God. You must be someone who can shed tears for God and can participate in wherever God goes with tears; that person will be most loved by God. It is the same principle.

Who is a friend of Jesus Christ? It is someone who has shed many tears for Jesus, someone who has cried for the path Jesus must take and the purpose of His providence. 

Who is a friend of Reverend Moon in the Unification Church? It is someone who has shed many tears of sympathy for Reverend Moon, standing in the same position. That is the principle. Therefore, in the future, those who shed many tears for the Unification Church will inherit that legacy.

The Unification Church must go beyond America, beyond the free world, and beyond the communist world; how pitiful is the Unification Church? How pitiful is Reverend Moon, who leads the Unification Church? How pitiful is God, who guides that organization? How pitiful is God, who leads and coaches that organization? Reverend Moon may have time to rest and sleep, but does God sleep? Reverend Moon may think of other things, but can God think of other things? Can the members of the Unification Church, who are before such God, be at ease? They are different. You must understand that you cannot even lift your face.

The Path of the Unification Church Must Go Through the Realm of Tears
The path that must go through the realm of tears is the path of the Unification Church! You must understand that. Each of you has taken responsibility for 360 households, right? Those in New York? "Yes." How many tears have you shed while visiting those homes? "God, since You cannot visit, I will visit in Your place with tears." Have you visited with that heart? You must visit with the heart that my tears, my sincerity, and my love are knocking on the doorknob. And while thinking from God's perspective, "It has taken me thousands of years to come to this house. I have walked the path of indemnity for thousands of years," you must think that way. Before speaking, you must be able to shed tears when you see their faces. Have you visited with such a heart? Did you do it reluctantly, thinking you should at least set a condition since the teacher told you to...? You must go with tears, true words, and true love. On the day that happens, you cannot extract this from that house. No matter how strong Satan is, as long as you cannot pull this out, you are being conquered.

When the morning sun rises, you must hang your tears and praise along with the 360 households, and visit with tears for all the birds flying in the neighborhood, the dogs running around, and all the people. I will visit in the morning, I will visit at lunch, I will visit in the evening, and I will visit at night! I will stay up all night for them, looking at the moon, looking at the stars, praying, and shedding tears; as long as such activities are happening, America and New York will not perish.

That is necessary. Now, have you visited all 360 households as the teacher said? Have you visited? Did you visit, or did you not? "Yes!" There are more people saying "no" than those saying "yes." Everyone must say "yes"!

Look. In the Exodus era, they received the command to "leave by a certain day!" Yet, the people of Israel had the responsibility to convey that message to every village and town, day and night, and if they failed to convey it, they would perish. On the day that the person who did not receive the message perishes, that person who failed to convey it will also perish. You must understand that they will perish forever. Even if all 360 households must live, if you fail to convey the message, you must understand that such a fate will be blocked. If your legs are tired, think that God is going to find His lost children and go while feeling tired and shedding tears. The 360 households must always be a place of tears where you go to wait and rest.

The Purpose of Placing You in New York
The teacher called this New York in America the front line. You must understand that this is the front line. Each of you has been entrusted with 360 households and made responsible; that is what I mean. And in this battle, you must understand that you are soldiers who have been commanded to bring about a victory of heart. The teacher cannot go alone, so I ask you to go in my place.

When you meet them, how much do you have to say? Reverend Moon has been beaten and has heard all sorts of insults and slander from the New York Times, the New York Daily News, the Washington Post, and others; how much do you think he has to say based on that? Placing you in the 360 households is not about your individual placement. It is about becoming the representative of the teacher and the representative of God.

At the same time as placing you, you must understand that some are spiritually instructed that "heavenly people will come." Can you sleep there without taking responsibility? Can you rest? Can you sleep, you guys? Can you do that? As America is perishing and the world is perishing, can you, as a young person in America, know the will and still sleep and rest? Can you still call yourself a Unification Church member and a child of God? You must repent. You must repent. If your legs are strong, you must break that leg of yours. You must understand that that head of yours is the head of Satan.

You must reveal this starting today. With such a heart, you must pray for the 360 households, just as Jesus prayed in the Garden of Gethsemane on behalf of the people of Israel. Therefore, you must cross the hill of tears, like the Garden of Gethsemane. You must save them through your death. It is easy to save and pass them on. You have the responsibility to restore them before the teacher and God. Can you eat, sleep, rest, and walk around shamelessly like that? I cannot do that. Did I do well, or did I do wrong? Think about it. Did I do well, or did I do wrong? "I did wrong." How will you stand before God in the spirit world after this? How will you stand before the teacher? If you cannot do that, do not eat! Do not drink! Do not sleep! You must understand that food will accuse you, sleep will accuse you, and clothes will accuse you. Do you not feel that? Have you never felt that? Do you not feel it?

Now, why must we do this? Why? Then we become the owners of love who can share love with the 360 households, owners of love. By sharing love with the 360 households, we become the owners who can resurrect life and love. Then when you go, you cannot treat them with disdain. On the day you do that, those people will become angry and lose their blessings. You must understand that such a battle has begun.

And the teacher gave out 30 copies of the Principle book and 30 sets of Principle lecture tapes, instructing you to change and distribute them every week; did you do that or not? Did you do it or not? "No, we did not." You must do it with tears, with tears! You must do it with tears! You must understand that many people are suffering to hear those words.
You must understand that there are people greater than you who are still asleep, not knowing this, just like you resolved to live in the name of God after hearing these words. Can't you do that? If you can't do that, can you go to heaven and become God's sons and daughters? Just as you must pass all the courses to graduate from a university, to enter the heavenly kingdom through the Unification Church and become God's sons and daughters, you must pass all those processes.

Think of New York as the front line and start anew. You said New York is the front line, but if you don't do it here, where will you do it? Who will do it? You must realize that the entire world is suffering because of you. It's not good for you to come here every morning and listen to the teacher's words. You must understand that it is a terrifying thing, a terrifying thing. If you do not act, you will be punished. You will be punished.

The teacher is not joking, not playing, not fooling around. You must understand that the tapes were made and the books were published while going into debt with nonexistent money. You must understand that not only the money of American people but also the money of Japanese and Korean members has been invested here for this purpose. I did this hoping that you would set an example.

If American youth do not do this, they will be cursed before Reverend Moon. The ones Reverend Moon hates and dislikes the most will be American youth, and the ones God hates and dislikes the most will also be American youth. That is the conclusion. If you had put the same sincerity that you put into this into underdeveloped countries like Africa, it would have been more than this. It would have been more than this. You must understand that the responsibility is heavy. Do you understand what I mean? "Yes."

You haven't done it all until now, right? If you had done all that and the Washington conference video tapes and the books written by Son Tak had all gone into homes, what would have happened? You would have been welcomed with great joy and weeping in New York City. When they see you, there will be weeping, weeping. The people of 360 homes would hold onto you and weep, wouldn't they? They would be glad and repent while shedding tears, wouldn't they? Think about it. I told you to expect all of that, but you guys! Haven't you taken responsibility for this?

So, what will happen? The sons and daughters of parents who opposed will be the first to come to the Unification Church for training. They see that there is a huge difference from what their mothers and fathers opposed.

Now, how many months has it been? It's the fifth month. So, should we do that or not? Think about it. Should we do it or not? "We must do it." Even if we can't eat, should we do this or not? Even if we can't sleep, should we do this or not? "We must do it." Which is more precious? Is sleeping precious, or is this precious? Is eating precious, or is this precious? "This is precious." Do you understand clearly? "Yes." From today, for the remaining three months, we must work day and night to make up for what we have not done until now.

So, should we do that or not? "We must do it." It must be done with tears, with tears. I can't just look at you and trust you. We must pray, pray. We must wake up at dawn and pray. I must struggle to fulfill the mission of the Messiah before the 360 homes and the mission of God, struggle. Just as God knows everything, I have the responsibility to know them thoroughly and save them. If there are difficulties in their homes, I must create an environment where they can come to me and say, "So-and-so! Our home is like this," and weep.

On the day this happens, New York will completely become what we want, and New York will become a lighthouse that can completely save America. We must understand that New York is the most evil city, the city of Satan. Therefore, we are on the front line, we are on the front line. We must turn this around. How many pairs of my shoes have fallen here, how much have my clothes been torn, how many tears have I shed? This is the competition, this is. There is no need to think of anything else, no other thoughts. We must worry about this more than eating or sleeping.

I thought that News World would be a good medium for broadcasting this work, which is why I instructed to sell News World. I understand that anyone can go into any house with a newspaper and that could happen. Looking at this, it seems to be falling down month by month. If you had put your sincerity into it, one-third would have already been surpassed. I believe that one-third is always surpassed. So, will you start doing this from this morning? "Yes."

Victory in New York is victory in America. If you try what the teacher tells you and it doesn't work, then you can stop, but you can't stop without even trying? The Unification Church itself will fail. It must be punished. Who must be punished? It should not be New York but the Unification Church itself. Since that cannot happen, we must take action.

Therefore, through these activities, we must shed tears, tears. We must shed tears with the teacher and join in the time of glory to shed tears with God. We must seek the path of restoration with tears, representing God's heart.

Stop making excuses, excuses. "Oh, I can't do it because I don't have money, I can't do it because I don't have a car." That's an excuse, an excuse. How big is Manhattan, New York? It's all small; I see that God has gathered us all here to do this work. It's all gathered in a small place. Do you understand what I mean? "Yes."

From today, without fail, we must do what we have not done until now, for the next three months... From today until New York turns around, if we set a standard for three years, it will completely turn around. Do you think that will happen or not? "I think it will." Do you think it will happen or not? Think about it. "I think it will." If you firmly believe that it will happen, you must understand that America will live and the world will live. You must do this for three years. You must do this until the 1980s. You are being told to do it here. Therefore, we cannot avoid this work. On the day we do this, the world will rise dramatically, and on the day we do not, the world will fall dramatically into hell.

That is why, from the perspective of God's will, we must understand that this is the front line. We must understand that this is a historically significant front line. Therefore, we must understand that this place has been declared the front line. Do you understand what I mean? "Yes." This applies to everyone, regardless of who they are. If your family hinders, obstructs, or interferes with this work, then abandon your family. If anything else becomes an obstacle to this work, throw it away. This is the only way America can win, and this will determine whether New York lives or dies. If it determines whether New York lives or dies, then it determines whether America lives or dies.

Ladies, do you see the prostitutes crawling at the end of 8th Avenue centered around the New Yorker Hotel in Manhattan? They are doing that all night long. We must do more than that, more than that. You women must completely resolve that with your hands, with your hands. You must understand that. So when men come, they should all be kicked in the side, and you should learn karate so that men cannot approach.

From now on, there is a lot of work to be done, from now on. For that work, New York City must cooperate with us. It cannot be done otherwise. Do you understand what I mean? "Yes." Now you understand clearly, clearly. You understand what the teacher is telling you to do. The teacher is serious about this, so he tells you not to eat and to do this work.

So, we must plant God's love along with tears, and we must plant truth and God's love. In doing so, neither the Unification Church nor New York nor America will fail. Who will take responsibility for this? Who? Can only God take responsibility? "No." Can only Reverend Moon take responsibility? "No." You too, you too. You must understand that you are also sad people who follow a sad God and a sad teacher. It is the same fate, the same fate. You must understand that if you cannot accomplish this, the fate of the world depends on this.

This kind of work has not been done throughout history until now. It is the first time, the first. That is why we are entering a new era. We are doing this work because the environment is ready to move when we attack.

So, knowing this, we must repent once again for not being able to take responsibility for this, and with tears in our eyes, we must resolve once again to walk the path of restoration in place of God's heart, based on the words of the teacher. Then, there will be songs of victory in your tears. Glory will come in tears, and there will surely be God's love and a reunion with God in tears. So, you must clearly understand the phrase "Let us return with tears." Memorize it. "Let us return with tears!" I hope for God's blessing. *
